***расхожий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расхожий.html>расхо́жий</a> (19370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́д</a>(и́ться)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasxod(ítʹsja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расхожий.html>расхо́жий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasxóžij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(goods)</i> in demand, <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in everyday use
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расхожий.html>расхо́жий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:костюм.html>костю́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasxóžij</b> kostjúm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">everyday/casual suit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расхожий.html>расхо́жее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражение.html>выраже́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasxóžeje</b> vyražénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">byword</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> common, widespread, commonplace, stock, stereotyped
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расхожий.html>расхо́жее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasxóžeje</b> mnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stereotyped view</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расхожий.html>расхо́жий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюжет.html>сюже́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasxóžij</b> sjužét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">commonplace/run-of-the-mill/hackneyed plot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***расхотеться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расхотеться.html>расхоте́ться</a> (21954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">расхоте́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasxotétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хри́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тан.html>тан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***расцветать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расцветать.html>расцвета́ть</a> (14901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">расцвет-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rascvet-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцветать.html>расцвета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rascvetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцвести.html>расцвести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blossom, to bloom <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">have or open into blossoms</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flourish, to thrive, to prosper</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расцветка.html>расцве́тка</a> (19232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cvet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцветка.html>расцве́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rascvétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцветка.html>расцве́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцветка.html>расцве́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцветка.html>расцве́ток</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> colours, colouration, colouring

***расценивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расценивать.html>расце́нивать</a> (17496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расценить.html>расцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rascenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расценивать.html>расце́нивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rascénivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расценить.html>расцени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to estimate, to value, to assess</li>
<li>to rate <i>(as)</i>, to consider, to regard <i>(as)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расценивать.html>расце́ниваю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оскорбление.html>оскорбле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>rascénivaju</b> éto kak oskorblénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I consider that an insult</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расценивать.html>расце́ниваете</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступление.html>выступле́ние</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak vy <b>rascénivajete</b> jevó vystuplénije?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what do you make/think of his speech?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ценить.html>цени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расчесать.html>расчеса́ть</a> (17961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чесать.html>чеса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">česátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчесать.html>расчеса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasčesátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчесывать.html>расчёсывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to comb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расчесать.html>расчеса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasčesátʹ</b> vólosy na probór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to part one's hair</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to card (flax or wool)</li>
<li>to scratch raw, to irritate by scratching</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, to defeat</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расчет.html>расчёт</a> (1827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчет.html>расчёт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasčót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчет.html>расчёта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчет.html>расчёты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчет.html>расчётов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчетный.html>расчётный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>calculation</li>
<li>estimation</li>
<li>payment, settlement of accounts</li>
<li>dismissal, firing, sack</li>
<li>consideration, account</li>
<li>intention, providence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gunners</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***расчистить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расчистить.html>расчи́стить</a> (15025)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчистить.html>расчи́стить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasčístitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расчищать.html>расчища́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clear, to clear away</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>стить</b>

Зализняка — 4a[②].      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:расчищать.html>расчища́ть</a>.
